# Acastina REED, 1927 — unnecessary_replacement: Acaste
# Acheilus RAYMOND, 1924 — preocc.: Peracheilus
# Acrectopyge HAWLE & CORDA, 1847 in VOGDES, 1925 — no family
# Actinobolus EICHWALD, 1858 — no family
# Actinolobus EICHWALD, 1858 — j.s.s.: Illaenus
# Actinopeltis POULSEN, 1946 — preocc.: Grinnellaspis
# Aeglina BARRANDE, 1850 — j.o.s.: Cyclopyge; replacement: Egle
# Aeonia BURMEISTER, 1843 — j.o.s.: Proetus
# Aliger HOWELL, 1937 — preocc.: Aligerites
# Alloctops RAFINESQUE, 1832 — no family
# Ambonslium KOBAYASHI, 1941 — no family
# Amphion PANDER, 1830 — preocc.: Pliomera
# Anderssonia SUN, 1924 — preocc.: Anderssonella
# Aneuacanthus BARRANDE, 1856 — no family
# Aneucanthus ANGELIN, 1854 — unnecessary_replacement: Acontheus and thus j.o.s. of Acontheus
# Anginouyia SAVITSKY et al., 1974 — no family
# Anisonotus RAYMOND, 1920 — preocc.: Anisonotella
